<!-- https://developers.home-assistant.io/docs/add-ons/presentation#keeping-a-changelog -->

## 1.2.200
- **Cursor step default: 15 min ŌåÆ 5 min.** v1.2.198 expanded the option set (1/2/3/4/5/10/12/15/30/60) and v1.2.199 wired the page to actually honor the saved value, but the default that fresh users land on was still 15 ŌĆö too coarse for the typical "land the cursor on a specific moment" workflow most users actually want. Bumped the default in three places (settings.html dropdown selected attr, settings.html `?? 15` fallback, rhythm-design.html `let cursorStepMin` initializer + `_stepCursor` fallback) and updated the webserver.py allowlist comment to match. Users who'd already saved a value are unaffected (config wins); only fresh / never-touched configs see the new default.
- **Sun intensity chip moved up out of the chart canvas, into a dedicated header strip above the cct-banner.** v1.2.197 placed the chip ON the chart canvas at `chart.offsetTop + 6` so it overlaid the very top of the plot area ("sun shining over the curve"). User feedback: that put it visually adjacent to the chart's "sun dimming" annotation, making the percentage read like the value of that annotation rather than an independent header. Fix: added `padding-top: 22px` to `#chart-shell` to reserve a strip ABOVE the cct-banner; chip now positions at `top: 4px` of chart-shell (default CSS, no per-frame JS), still anchored at solar-noon x via `xToPx`. Popover anchor moved from `chart.offsetTop + 28` to a static `top: 24px` for the same reason. Net: chip reads as a sibling header element of "Sun intensity %" ŌĆö with the cct-banner directly below it and the chart further below ŌĆö rather than as part of the chart's annotation layer.
- **Master reset (Ōå║) recolored orange-on-dark to stand out as actionable.** v1.2.198 already hid the button when the chart view is clean (no-op state), but when visible it was `background: rgba(0,0,0,0.22) / color: inherit` ŌĆö same dark-translucent treatment as the row 2 ŌåÉ/ŌåÆ arrows, so it blended in. Now `background: rgba(0,0,0,0.45) / border: 1px solid rgba(254,172,96,0.45) / color: var(--accent)` ŌĆö orange Ōå║ on darkened bg with a soft orange ring, mirroring the home page power button's accent-on-dark treatment. Hover lifts to a tinted orange wash (`rgba(254,172,96,0.18)` bg + full accent border + accent-hover ink). The orange flags "this button does something page-scope" against the surrounding CCT-tinted banner, regardless of whether that tint is warm-amber (mid-day) or cool-blue (deep night).

## 1.2.199
- **Cursor step bugfix: rhythm-design page never read `rhythm_cursor_step_min` from the server.** v1.2.198 added the 1/2/3/4/12 min options but the cursor still moved by 15 min regardless of the user's pick. Root cause: `loadConfig()` (which reads `data.rhythm_cursor_step_min` and assigns `cursorStepMin`) is defined but was never called during `DOMContentLoaded` init ŌĆö the page only consumes a small subset of `window.circadianData.config` (lat/lon/timezone/use_ha_location). Added `rhythm_cursor_step_min` to the injected-config copy list and assigned `cursorStepMin` from it on init. Also: `_stepCursor` now reads `config.rhythm_cursor_step_min` directly each call as a fresh-fallback (covers cases where `cursorStepMin` is stale), and a new `pageshow` listener calls `loadConfig()` on bfcache restore so navigating back from Settings picks up a freshly-saved cursor step without a hard reload.
- **Wake/bed speed slider: redefined transition durations to user-friendly targets.** Old slot durations were `~14.7h / 9.8h / 7.4h / 5.9h / 4.5h / 3.5h / 2.6h / 2.0h / 1.5h / 1.07h / 11.8min / 5.9min` ŌĆö uneven, no clean round numbers. New target ladder: `10h / 7.5h / 5.5h / 4h / 3h / 2.25h / 1.5h / 1h / 30min / 15min / 5min / 2min`. Recomputed `SPEED_TO_SLOPE` from `k = 5.889 / hours` so the displayed durations come out exact (Plotly curve shape now matches what the readout claims). Tightened `speedTransitionLabel` formatter to strip trailing zeros so `4.0 ŌåÆ "4 hr"`, `7.5 ŌåÆ "7.5 hr"`, `2.25 ŌåÆ "2.25 hr"` all read clean instead of `4.0`/`2.3`. Same 12 word labels (CalmŌĆ”Instant) preserved.
- **"Try it" ŌåÆ "Experience" rename in banner row 2 right slot.** Same Live Design entry point, clearer label ("Try" implied transient, "Experience" carries the "see what these settings actually look like in your room" intent better). Also tightened banner spacing for mobile: `.cct-banner-arrows` gap `6 ŌåÆ 3px` (ŌåÉ/time/ŌåÆ cluster reads as one unit), and the Experience button's iconŌåÆlabel gap `6 ŌåÆ 4px` (with `padding-right` trimmed `12 ŌåÆ 11px` to compensate) so the beacon icon sits visually attached to the label rather than floating.
- **Wake/bed pill connector: dynamic height, lands ON the x-axis line (not below the tick labels).** v1.2.198's hardcoded `28px` only reached chart-shell coord 70 (chart's bottom edge), which is BELOW the Plotly x-tick labels (3a/6a/...) ŌĆö visually they stopped short of the axis. Now compute `axisFromShellBottom = chartShell.offsetHeight - chart.offsetTop - yaxis._offset - yaxis._length` against Plotly's `_fullLayout` and set `--phase-connector-h` per-frame in `positionOverlays()` so the connector top meets the axis line exactly, regardless of Plotly's bottom margin.
- **Sunrise/sunset get the same connector treatment.** Added `.solar-label::before` (1px-wide sun-tinted hairline) bridging from the label up to the x-axis line, height set per-frame from the same `axisFromShellBottom` math (offset for the label being above its own bottom). Plus dropped `.solar-label { bottom: 65 ŌåÆ 50px }` so the labels sit cleanly BELOW the x-tick labels (no longer kissing 3a/6a/9a) and the new connector has room to extend.
- **Sun-dimming reference line + label muted a touch.** The dotted "room target above sun-dimmed bulb output" line was `width: 1.4 / rgba(220,220,220,0.6)` and the "sun dimming" annotation was `size: 9 / alpha 0.7`. Both nudged down so they sit clearly behind the primary brightness curve rather than competing with it: line `width: 1.2 / alpha 0.42`, annotation `size: 8 / alpha 0.5`.
- **Page header: rhythm zone name bumped + visually centered, RHYTHM ZONE chip scrunched.** Name input went `font-size: var(--font-display)` (1.1rem) ŌåÆ `1.25rem` and `weight: 600 ŌåÆ 700`, with `line-height: 1.1` so it has visual presence; `.rhythm-name-group` got `justify-content: center` so the name+chip stack centers vertically against the back button. Chip went `font-size: 0.54rem ŌåÆ 0.48rem`, `padding: 1px 6px ŌåÆ 0 5px`, `border-radius: 10px ŌåÆ 8px`, `opacity: 0.55 ŌåÆ 0.5` ŌĆö tighter and quieter so the name dominates.
- **Home page zone header: chip moved between name and phase line.** Was `name ŌåÆ phase-label (Bed at 10p) ŌåÆ RHYTHM ZONE chip`. Now `name ŌåÆ RHYTHM ZONE chip ŌåÆ phase-label` so the type label reads as a sub-label directly under the zone name (matching the rhythm-design page's `name ŌåÆ chip` stack), and the phase line ("bed/wake at HH:MM") slots naturally beneath as the third row of context.

## 1.2.198
- **Cursor step: added 1, 2, 3, 4, 12 min options.** Settings ŌåÆ App ŌåÆ Rhythm chart ŌåÆ Cursor step now offers `1 / 2 / 3 / 4 / 5 / 10 / 12 / 15 / 30 / 60` min instead of just `5 / 10 / 15 / 30 / 60`. The fine-grained low end (1ŌĆō4 min) lets users land the chart cursor on a specific moment during transitions where lights are changing fast (around wake/bed boundaries); 12 min slots in for users who want a 5-tap-per-hour cadence. ŌåÉ/ŌåÆ on the banner already honor this setting via `_stepCursor` reading `cursorStepMin` (loaded from `rhythm_cursor_step_min` config), no JS changes needed.
- **Banner Ōå║ master reset hidden when there's nothing to reset.** Previously visible at all times in row 1 right corner, even immediately after page load when the chip would be a no-op. New `isChartViewDirty()` returns true if any of: cursor not tracking now, outdoor source overridden from `current`, wake/bed dragged but unsaved, or month chip set to a non-current month. `updateBannerResetVisibility()` toggles `display: none` on `#cct-banner-reset` based on that check, and is called from `positionOverlays()` so it tracks live state changes. `grid-template-columns: 1fr auto` on row 1 means the readout reflows full-width when the reset disappears, no layout hole.
- **Cursor extender top gap closed; bottom now meets Plotly's plot area exactly.** v1.2.197 positioned the extender from `bannerBottom ŌåÆ chartTop`, but Plotly's `_fullLayout.yaxis._offset` (top margin inside the chart div) left a few pixels of dark space below the extender bottom and above where Plotly actually starts drawing the cursor line ŌĆö visible as a seam. Fix: extender top now overlaps the banner by 3px (kills the visible top seam from subpixel rendering / banner edge anti-aliasing), and extender bottom = `chart.offsetTop + yaxis._offset` (lands exactly at the top of the plot area so it meets Plotly's cursor line with no gap). Net: continuous CCT-tinted thread from banner readout straight down to the ball on the curve.
- **Wake/bed connector line capped at the x-axis (no more pierce into the chart).** v1.2.197 used `height: 60px` on `.phase-handle::before` which placed the connector top ~32px above the x-axis, visibly cutting into the chart canvas. Recomputed against actual chart-shell math (padding-bottom 70px, handle bottom 14px, handle height 34px, connector starts 6px into the pill via `bottom: calc(100% - 6px)`) ŌåÆ connector base sits at 42px from chart-shell bottom, so `height: 28px` lands the top exactly at the x-axis (70 - 42 = 28).
- **Sunrise/sunset prominence raised to match the sun-intensity chip.** v1.2.197 deliberately muted them (9px / alpha 0.65) on the theory that the chip should be "the" focal sun-cluster element. User feedback: the three should read at equal weight ŌĆö they're all the sun cluster, no member is more important than the others. Bumped `.solar-label` to `font-size: 11px`, `font-weight: 600`, `color: rgba(255,225,140,0.92)`, `font-variant-numeric: tabular-nums` ŌĆö exactly matches `.outdoor-chip` so all three sun elements (sunrise, sun-intensity chip, sunset) read as one consistent cluster.
- **"Sun angle response" sub-subsection styling: clearer title-vs-fields hierarchy.** v1.2.197's `.sub-subsection-title` (0.78rem, --muted, uppercase letter-spaced 0.04em) blended visually with the two `.tune-control-row` field labels below it, reading as 3 equal-weight rows instead of one header + two fields. Bumped title to `0.92rem`, `font-weight: 700`, `color: var(--text)` (not muted), `letter-spacing: 0.01em` (not uppercase), and added `padding-bottom: 6px` + `border-bottom: 1px solid var(--line)` so the title visually anchors above the fields with a clear separator. Sub-subsection container padding bumped slightly (`8px 0 4px 10px ŌåÆ 10px 0 4px 12px`) and meta tag font sized up (`0.72rem ŌåÆ 0.78rem`, `var(--muted2) ŌåÆ var(--muted)`) to balance the heavier title.

## 1.2.197
- **Banner contrast fix: month chip + Try-it inherit ink color from CCT tint.** Both buttons had hardcoded light-gray text + white-tinted borders that washed out against bright/warm banner tints (around mid-day amber). Switched both to `color: inherit` + `border: 1px solid currentColor` + `background: rgba(0,0,0,0.18)`, so they pick up the banner's `readableTextColor(rgb)` (black on warm tints, white on cool tints) and stay legible across the full CCT range. Removed the obsolete try-it `backdrop-filter` since the banner background is now opaque.
- **Sun intensity chip moved ONTO chart canvas (dark Plotly bg) instead of into the gap above.** Was floating in the lighter card-color gap between banner and chart, which made it look like it belonged to the banner. Now positioned at `chart.offsetTop + 6px` so it overlays the very top of the plot area, matching the visual model of "sun shining over the curve" ŌĆö the chip's dark surroundings are now the chart's canvas, same surface as the curve itself. Popover top adjusted to `chart.offsetTop + 28px` to land just below the chip.
- **Wake/bed handles dropped from `bottom: 32px` ŌåÆ `bottom: 14px`; connector line raised 50px ŌåÆ 60px.** v1.2.196 collided with sunrise/sunset because the labels moved up while the pills stayed put. Pills now sit lower in the chart-shell bottom margin with breathing room from the solar labels above; the longer connector line keeps the pill anchored to the x-axis at the new height.
- **Sunrise/sunset labels: smaller (10px ŌåÆ 9px) and more muted (alpha 0.78 ŌåÆ 0.65).** Bookend the sun-cluster but don't compete with the focal sun-intensity chip ŌĆö the chip is "the" sun-cluster element, sunrise/sunset are the supporting context.
- **Bed-side chart coloring flipped to blue (matching bed pill).** `DESCEND_COLORS` was still amber/yellow (`#ffe680`, `rgba(255,220,100,0.12)` shade, `rgba(255,230,128,0.85)` boundary). Switched to `#6fa9ff` text/hoverBg, `rgba(111,169,255,0.18)` shade, `rgba(111,169,255,0.85)` boundary, `rgba(111,169,255,0.75)` axis ŌĆö same palette as the bed pill. Sleep cluster (wake = ascend sky-blue, bed = descend deeper-blue) now reads as one cool family on the chart, not split across blue + yellow.
- **Cursor line CCT-tinted instead of white, extending up through the gap into the banner.** White cursor line broke the visual continuity between the CCT-tinted banner readout and the CCT-tinted ball on the curve. Line color now derives from `cctToRGB(cursorPoint.cct)` (matches the ball + banner). New `.cursor-extender` HTML overlay div bridges the gap between banner-bottom and chart-top, also CCT-tinted, so the column reads as one continuous "current moment" thread: banner readout ŌåÆ extender ŌåÆ in-chart line ŌåÆ ball ŌåÆ wake/bed handles below. Positioned in `positionOverlays()` from `xToPx(visHour(cursorHour, xA))`.
- **"Sun angle response" reorganized as a sub-subsection of "Sun dimming".** Was a sibling block in the brightness sub-section with its own border-top and inline styles. Moved inside `#brightness-sensitivity-body` so it visually nests under "Sun dimming". New `.sub-subsection` CSS class (left border, indented, smaller uppercase title with muted meta tag) replaces the old inline divider so the parent-child hierarchy reads cleanly without adding a third card-style box.

## 1.2.196
- **Rhythm Designer chart: edge-to-edge CCT-tinted banner replaces the chart-chrome row + cursor chip.** The whole banner IS the cursor controller now ŌĆö its background tint follows cursor CCT (not just a small chip's). Two rows: row 1 holds a large `% ┬Ę K` readout (focal, CCT-tinted) and the `Ōå║` master reset in the right corner (page-scope, not time-scope, visually separated from the time arrows so its broader reach reads correctly). Row 2 holds the month chip (left), `ŌåÉ time ŌåÆ` cluster (centered, preserves the eyes-on-lights muscle memory of fixed arrow positions), and Try-it (right). `.chart-chrome` / `.cursor-chip*` CSS + HTML deleted; `.cct-banner*` CSS + HTML replaces it. `positionOverlays` now writes the readout/time/CCT tint into the new banner element. `cursor-chip-reset` / `cursor-chip-prev` / `cursor-chip-next` click bindings retargeted to `cct-banner-reset` / `cct-banner-prev` / `cct-banner-next`. `#chart-section` overrides section-block padding to 0 so the banner spans card edge-to-edge; chart shell padding adjusted to match.
- **Sun intensity: chip simplified to `ŌśĆ 60%` and moved ABOVE the chart at solar noon ("sun shining over the graph").** Was at the bottom (between sunrise/sunset). The inline "Sun intensity" text label that v1.2.194 added is dropped ŌĆö the chip is now icon + percent only. "Sun intensity" surfaces as a prominent header (13px / 700 weight) inside the popover that opens on tap. The chip's top is computed in `positionOverlays` against `chart.offsetTop` so it nestles in a 22px gap added between the banner and the chart canvas; left position still uses `xToPx(solarNoon)`. Together with sunrise/sunset (also retinted yellow) the three form a sun-arc visual: sun above + sunrise/sunset bookending below.
- **Color flip: sleep cluster blue, sun cluster yellow.** Bed pill changed from amber (`#ffe680`) to blue (`#6fa9ff`, slightly deeper than wake's `#5cb3ff` for differentiation), with matching connector line + ghost border updates. Bed-ink also flipped to dark blue. Wake stays its sky blue. Sunrise/sunset labels changed from muted gray (`rgba(215,215,215,0.75)`) to soft yellow (`rgba(255,225,140,0.78)`), and the sun-intensity chip text + icon switched to yellow as well. Result: sleep things (wake/bed pills) read as one cool cluster, sun things (sunrise/sunset/intensity) read as one warm cluster ŌĆö clearer visual grouping than the prior wake-blue / bed-yellow split.
- **Drop wake/bed auto-save on drag-end ŌåÆ drag is now preview-only.** Reversed the v1.2.194 auto-save direction. Per user: "i want to be able to play with the levers but not have it impact my home's schedule, unless i consciously change it." Drag-end no longer commits to today's group; the working drag value persists in `chartState.{wake|bed}DragVal` and the saved `config.{wake|bed}_time` is untouched. The 5-second undo chip + `_undoState` / `showUndoChip` / `hideUndoChip` / `undoLastSave` / `setupHandleActions` machinery is fully removed (no auto-save = nothing to undo).
- **New Sleep card "dirty bar" surfaces dragged values with explicit Save/Revert.** Replaces the dropped undo chip as the persistence affordance. When wake or bed is dragged on the chart, a bar appears at the top of the Sleep card body showing `WAKE 7:00a ŌåÆ 7:30a` (or `BED ...`) with `[Revert]` and `[Save]` buttons. Save commits to today's group via `commitSave(kind, groupForToday(kind).id)` (preserves alt-day clusters); Revert clears the drag value. If both wake and bed are dragged, the bar shows whichever was most recently moved and Save commits both in one shot. `updateSleepDirtyBar` is invoked from `positionOverlays` so the bar tracks live drag state. Master reset (banner Ōå║) clears drag values + the bar (schedule never changed).
- **Vertical padding crush on chart card.** `.section-block` padding override for `#chart-section` removes the 10px/8px vertical padding so the new banner sits flush at the top edge and the chart's bottom solar band doesn't get a duplicate gap.

## 1.2.195
- **Hotfix: `get_area_status` NameError on `outdoor_norm` (regression from v1.2.188).** The v1.2.188 sun-times consolidation deleted the local `outdoor_norm = lux_tracker.get_outdoor_normalized()` / `outdoor_source = lux_tracker.get_outdoor_source()` block from `get_area_status` (and two sibling paths) when it switched to delegating to `self.client._get_sun_times()`. The two sibling paths were either fine (no later reference to those locals) or re-defined `outdoor_norm` themselves further down. But `get_area_status` references both names in five places after the deletion (sun_bright_factor compute at line ~3004, status payload `outdoor_normalized` / `outdoor_source` / `outdoor_source_entity` / `sun_factor` at ~3227-3248), so every Area Status request after the consolidation raised `NameError: name 'outdoor_norm' is not defined`. Fix: pull both fields out of `sun_times` (the resolver already attaches them via `SunTimes.outdoor_normalized` / `outdoor_source`, fresh on every call ŌĆö `_get_sun_times` reads `lux_tracker` even on cache hits) into locals right after the sun_times resolution, restoring the same names the rest of the function expects. Two-line addition. No semantic change vs the pre-v1.2.188 version: same source (`lux_tracker.get_outdoor_normalized` / `get_outdoor_source` with None ŌåÆ 0.0/"none" coercion), just routed through the consolidated resolver instead of inlined. Caught from production logs (`[Area Status] Error: name 'outdoor_norm' is not defined` repeating every few seconds as the homepage polled the endpoint).

## 1.2.194
- **Rhythm-design chart card: tighter chrome, integrated master reset, auto-save wake/bed with undo, "Sun intensity" rename, "Rhythm Zone" sub-chip in header, padding crush.** Six coordinated changes that reclaim vertical and horizontal space on the chart card while making the controls more legible and self-explanatory. **(1) Page header restructure** ŌĆö drops the `Rhythm zone:` prefix label and adopts the home-page zone pattern: `Daily Rhythm 1` (as the editable name) with a small uppercase `RHYTHM ZONE` sub-chip beneath it (mirrors `.zone-type-chip` from `areas.html`: 0.54rem, 1px currentColor border, opacity 0.55, padding 1px 6px, border-radius 10px). New `.rhythm-name-group` column-flex wrapper aligns the name and sub-chip flush-left. **(2) Cursor chip restructure with master reset** ŌĆö the chip is now narrower and the time-of-cursor moves to row 2, sandwiched between the step arrows. Row 1: `% ┬Ę K` (color and brightness only, CCT-tinted). Row 2: `[Ōå║ reset] [ŌåÉ prev] [time] [ŌåÆ next]` ŌĆö the new master reset button is the leftmost item, visually attached to the cursor controls (zero ambiguity with the month chip a few pixels left). The `Jump to now` button is gone; its functionality is subsumed by the master reset, which does more. `resetChartView()` reverts the page to its "as-just-loaded" state for transient view controls: cursor ŌåÆ now (resumes live tracking), outdoor source ŌåÆ `current` (live weather), wake/bed drag working values ŌåÆ null (handles snap back to saved positions), month ŌåÆ current month, plus hides any visible undo chips and re-renders. It does NOT roll back saved config ŌĆö the page-load default IS today's saved config, so resetting view ŌēĀ undoing edits. The calendar emoji also leaves the month chip (just `April` text now ŌĆö the icon was redundant alongside the month name). `min-width: 180px ŌåÆ 150px` on the cursor chip; new `.cursor-chip-time` (44px min-width, tabular-nums, opacity 0.95) and `.cursor-chip-reset` (22px, Ōå║) selectors. **(3) "Sun intensity" rename** ŌĆö the bottom-row outdoor-conditions chip now reads `ŌśĆ Sun intensity 100%` (added `<span class="outdoor-chip-label">Sun intensity</span>` between the icon and percentage), and the popover gets a top-row `Sun intensity` title bar (uppercase 11px, muted2, with a bottom border separator) so when it opens it's unambiguous what's being adjusted. Same picker UX, just labeled. **(4) Auto-save wake/bed on drag-end with 5s undo** ŌĆö dragging a wake or bed pill and releasing now auto-commits to today's cluster (`groupForToday(kind).id` ŌĆö primary or alt) and shows a `Ōå║ undo` chip below the pill for 5 seconds. Tapping undo restores the full pre-drag snapshot of all four time slots (`wake_time`, `wake_alt_time`, `wake_alt_days`, plus the bed equivalents) so multi-key saves like `'all'` revert atomically rather than just clearing the dragged kind. The old `.handle-actions` row (Save Ō¢Š + Reset chips that appeared on dirty state) is gone ŌĆö multi-cluster saves (weekend, all-days) now belong to the Sleep card body, where they were always easier to express anyway. The chart-side save was overkill for the common case: drag, release, done. New `_undoState` per-kind keeps the prev snapshot + setTimeout handle; `showUndoChip()` / `hideUndoChip()` / `undoLastSave()` replace `openSavePopover()` / `resetWakeOrBed()`. `setupHandleDrag()`'s `end` handler now compares dragVal vs savedVal and either commits-then-shows-undo or just clears the drag working copy (no-op drags don't trigger a save). Outside-click and chart-pointerdown selectors updated from `.handle-actions` / `.action-chip` to `.handle-undo` / `.undo-chip`. **(5) Crush rhythm-card horizontal padding** ŌĆö `.section-block` padding `10px 16px 8px ŌåÆ 10px 6px 8px` reclaims ~20px on each side of the chart card, giving the graph room to breathe and unwrapping the Try-it label without needing a `nowrap` rule. **(6) Skip the `nowrap` patch on Try-it** ŌĆö between the thinner cursor chip (no more `Jump to now`) and the crushed horizontal padding, there's enough room for `Try it` to render on a single line at all viewport widths the rhythm chart is usable on; no defensive CSS needed. Net: chart card is shorter (no Save/Reset row eats vertical space below the pill until needed), wider in usable horizontal space, and the controls that ARE present are each labeled with their actual function rather than icon-only. Changes confined to `addon/rhythm-design.html` (HTML structure, ~140 lines of CSS deltas, ~80 lines of JS deltas ŌĆö readout text format, drag-end auto-save, undo chip lifecycle, master reset).

## 1.2.193
- **Chart card chrome zone: month chip (left), fixed cursor chip with ŌåÉ/Jump-to-now/ŌåÆ controls (center), Try-it (right). New "Cursor step" setting.** Restructures the rhythm-design chart card to give the cursor chip a dedicated, fixed-position home above the curve canvas ŌĆö solves three concurrent collisions from v1.2.192 (cursor chip overlapping the curve at 100% max-bri, cursor chip overlapping the "sun dimming" annotation at peak, Try-it sitting on top of the month chip in the top-right corner) and unlocks ergonomic tap-without-looking control. Five coordinated changes across `addon/rhythm-design.html`, `addon/settings.html`, and `addon/webserver.py`. **(1) New `.chart-chrome` flex/grid row** at the top of `#chart-shell`, `min-height: 58px`, three slots via `grid-template-columns: 1fr auto 1fr` so the center slot is dead-centered regardless of left/right widths. Curve canvas (`#chart`) shifts down by ~58px in normal flow; bottom-anchored items (sunrise/sunset labels, outdoor chip, wake/bed pills, ghosts, action chips ŌĆö all positioned with `bottom:` rather than `top:`) are unaffected. Chart-shell `padding-top: 8px ŌåÆ 0` (chrome row owns its own spacing now). **(2) Cursor chip rewrite ŌĆö fixed position, fixed dimensions, 2 rows.** Old floating `.now-pill` (positioned at `xToPx(cursorHour)` with anchor-pivot zones + drop-on-conflict logic for collisions with month chip) replaced by a static `.cursor-chip` in the chrome row's center slot. Row 1: `time ┬Ę % ┬Ę K` readout (CCT-tinted background/border, same `cctToRGB` + `colorWithAlpha` + `readableTextColor` palette as before). Row 2: `ŌåÉ [Jump to now] ŌåÆ`. The chip's POSITION never changes as the cursor scrubs ŌĆö only its content (readout text + tint colors) updates. The cursor LINE on the chart still moves under your thumb as you scrub; the chip stays put so the arrow buttons live in muscle memory and you can tap them while watching the lights, not the phone. Jump-to-now button is `disabled` (low-opacity, non-clickable) when `cursorTrackingNow === true` so the width stays stable but you can't waste a tap. Removed: the entire ~50-line anchor-pivot/drop-on-conflict block in `positionOverlays()` (was lines ~4144-4176, became ~16 lines that just update the chip's readout + tint). **(3) ŌåÉ/ŌåÆ arrow handlers ŌĆö step cursor by configurable amount.** New `_stepCursor(dirSign)` helper converts `cursorHour` to chart-frame coordinates via `visHour(cursorHour, xA)`, adds `┬▒(stepMin/60)` hours, clamps to `[xA, xA + 24 - 0.001]` (matches the v1.2.189 right-edge clamp pattern ŌĆö cursor doesn't wrap from the right edge to the left, which would visually look like a teleport across the whole chart), then `wrapHour()` back to wall-clock 0-24 frame for `cursorHour`. Sets `cursorTrackingNow = false` and calls `applyCursor()` (which already broadcasts to active Try-it areas via `applyLiveLight`, so stepping while in Try-it mode pulses the lights). Step amount sourced from new `cursorStepMin` global (default 15), populated from `/api/config` in `loadConfig()`. **(4) Cursor step setting ŌĆö Settings ŌåÆ App ŌåÆ Rhythm chart sub-divider.** New `<select id="rhythm-cursor-step-min">` with options 5/10/15/30/60 min, default 15. Lives in the App section under a new "Rhythm chart" sub-divider (mirrors the existing "Homepage" sub-divider pattern). Wired to load/save/listener triplet alongside `home_slider_mode` / `home_buttons_mode`. Config key `rhythm_cursor_step_min` added to `webserver.py` `GLOBAL_SETTINGS` allowlist so the POST `/api/config` accepts and persists it. Default 15 chosen because: matches typical lighting-program granularity, gives 4 taps per hour (digestible), and aligns with how scheduling is generally framed in HA (15-min slots in calendars / automations). Smaller values (5, 10) for users who want fine "see the lights at 4:15 vs 4:30" tuning; larger (30, 60) for users who want to skim the whole day quickly. **(5) Try-it + month chip relocation.** Both buttons drop their `position: absolute / top / right` anchors and become normal-flow children of the chart-chrome row's right and left slots respectively. Their popovers (`.try-it-popover`, `.month-popover`) remain `position: absolute` inside `chart-shell` but with new anchor offsets (`top: 60px` for both ŌĆö chrome row + 4px gap; `right: 10px` for try-it popover, `left: 10px` for month popover) so they pop down from their new anchors rather than from the old top-right corner. The previously-needed CSS quirks (`.try-it-btn` with `position:absolute; top:8px; right:8px; z-index:10`) are gone ŌĆö a cleaner DOM, one less layer of z-index stacking concerns. **What this enables next:** with cursor chip out of the curve area, the top-center of the chart (around solar noon) is finally clean enough to host the outdoor conditions chip in a "sun arc" layout (sunrise bottom-left, conditions overhead, sunset bottom-right). Deferred to a follow-up so this ship stays focused on the chrome zone + cursor controls. **Net code:** rhythm-design.html ~+90/-110 lines (new `.chart-chrome` + `.cursor-chip` CSS, new chrome-row HTML wrapper, drops the old now-pill div and its ~50-line positionOverlays anchor-pivot block, adds `_stepCursor` + Jump-to-now handlers, adds `cursorStepMin` global + load wiring, drops position:absolute from `.try-it-btn` and `.month-chip`); settings.html +24 lines (Rhythm chart sub-divider with the cursor step dropdown + load/save/listener); webserver.py +1 line (allowlist entry). config.yaml + build.yaml version bump to 1.2.193.

## 1.2.192
- **Settings "Sun" section + optional zone-level Sun angle response controls + Live Design relabeled "Try it" with multi-area broadcast (max 3) inside the chart card + small label/cursor polish.** Five coordinated UI changes across `addon/settings.html`, `addon/rhythm-design.html`, and `addon/webserver.py`. **(1) Settings "Location" ŌåÆ "Sun" section** with a new "Sun angle response" sub-divider wrapping the existing `sun_saturation` (% of peak elevation) + `sun_saturation_ramp` (linear/squared) fields. Adds a new home-wide `show_sun_angle_in_zone` checkbox (default off): when off, those fields live only in Settings; when on, they ALSO surface in the rhythm-zone Brightness card so users can see the live curve respond as they tune. Note in the popover header: "applies to all zones, also affects sun cooling" ŌĆö the same `outdoor_normalized` value flows through both `pipeline.py` brightness multiplier and `brain.py` daylight CCT blend, so adjusting these in either UI changes both vectors. POSTs `{sun_saturation, sun_saturation_ramp}` to `/api/config`, mutates `_outdoorParams`, calls `renderChart()` + `applyCursor()` for live feedback. `webserver.py` GLOBAL_SETTINGS allowlist + `/api/outdoor-status` payload extended with `show_sun_angle_in_zone`. **(2) "Sun contribution" annotation ŌåÆ "Sun dimming"** on the rhythm-design chart (line ~3631) ŌĆö the inline label hugging the dotted reference curve now matches the Brightness card's "Sun dimming" sub-section header for terminology consistency. The variable name `sunContribAnchor` left unchanged (no UI impact). **(3) Sunrise/sunset solar label cursor `help` ŌåÆ `default`** (line 502) ŌĆö hovering "sunrise" or "sunset" labels on the chart no longer turns the cursor into a question mark; they're informational labels not interactive tooltips. **(4) Live Design moved INTO chart card + relabeled "Try it" with hidden popover (progressive disclosure).** Removed the above-chart `<div class="live-design-controls">` row, the `<div class="live-pip">` overlay, the `<div class="live-fab">` overlay, and all `.live-design-*`/`.live-pip-*`/`.live-fab-*`/`@keyframes live-pulse|fab-glow|live-pip-pulse` CSS. The button starts as "Try it" with a broadcast icon; while active it pulses (`@keyframes try-it-glow` on `.try-it-btn.is-live`) and the label morphs through `_formatAreaLabel(ids)`: 1 area ŌåÆ "Trying in [Area]", 2 areas ŌåÆ "Trying in [A] + [B]", 3 areas ŌåÆ "Trying in [A] +2". Click the active button to reopen the popover (Stop button visible inside). Click outside dismisses. **(5) Multi-area broadcast capped at 3** (Zigbee-friendly). New JS state: `liveDesignAreaIds = []` (was singular `liveDesignAreaId`), `liveDesignAreas = []` (cache), `TRY_IT_MAX = 3`. The popover header shows a live `0/3` counter; rows above the cap render `is-disabled`. `commitTryItSelection()` computes added/removed deltas vs. the previous active set so circadian suppression is only toggled per-area on actual transitions (not all-on-every-commit). `applyLiveLight()` fans out via `Promise.all(ids.map(...))`. `sendLiveDesignHeartbeat(areaIds)`/`startLiveDesignHeartbeat(areaIds)` take an array snapshot and broadcast to all selected areas at the 30s interval. The server-side 60s watchdog applies per-area as before. `stopTryIt()` and the standalone `stopLiveDesign()` (called from `goBack`/`beforeunload`) re-enable circadian for ALL currently-active areas via the same `Promise.all` pattern. ## 1.2.191
- **Tighten 2-step CT trigger and lengthen Phase 1 hold so color settles before brightness ramps.** Two coordinated changes hitting both 2-step turn-on paths (per-area in `main.py:_deliver_filtered`, batch in `primitives.py._dispatch_to_batches`). **(1) CT threshold default 500K ŌåÆ 200K** at `main.py:3825` and `primitives.py:4288`. The prior 500K bar meant warm-shift transitions in the 200ŌĆō500K range (e.g. 867K ŌåÆ 1212K from the 06:28 living-room turn-on) skipped 2-step entirely and fired a single direct command; the bulb's bright-then-dim hardware boot artifact was the visible result. 200K catches those mid-range CT swings. **(2) Phase 1 transition extended to match `two_step_delay`, with a full hold on top.** Previously P1 used the input `transition` arg (typically 0.4s for switch presses) and the inter-phase sleep was a single `delay`; the 0.5s sleep barely outlasted the 0.4s transition, leaving almost no settled-color window before P2 ramped brightness. New behavior: P1 transition = `_get_two_step_delay()` (the user-configurable "delay between steps" setting), and `asyncio.sleep(delay * 2)` between waves ŌĆö so P1 spends `delay` interpolating to 1% (or low-bri/dim target), then the bulb holds at that settled state for another `delay`, then P2 fires with the original `transition` for the brightness ramp. Total wait from P1 fire to P2 fire = `2 * delay`. Default 5 tenths ŌåÆ P1 transitions for 0.5s, holds for 0.5s, P2 fires at the 1.0s mark. P2 transition unchanged (still uses input `transition`). This affects all 2-step paths uniformly: brighten, dim, offŌåÆon (per-area and batched). For offŌåÆon the 0ŌåÆ1% transition is still visually imperceptible regardless of duration; the longer hold just gives the bulb more time to fully render the target color before the brightness ramp begins. The three non-turn-on consumers of `_get_two_step_delay()` (feedback cue at `main.py:2867`, `_bounce_at_limit` at `primitives.py:4521`, `alert_bounce` at `primitives.py:4685`) are unchanged ŌĆö they're visual-effect timers, not 2-step turn-on.

## 1.2.190
- **Revert solid/dotted swap from v1.2.189 + align Live Design broadcast with the visible (sun-dimmed) curve** ŌĆö v1.2.189 made solid = `roomTargetPct` (calculated, un-dimmed) and dotted = `brightnessPct` (sun-dimmed). User feedback after seeing it in production: the better mental model is **solid = what the bulb actually outputs = what the cursor reads = what Live Design broadcasts to the lights**, with the dotted reference above showing what the rhythm WOULD prescribe without the sun's contribution. Three coordinated changes in `addon/rhythm-design.html`. **(1) Curve assignments restored:** filled+colored line segments back to `brightnessPct` for `y0`/`y1` (the visible bulb-output curve gets the cct gradient + fill); dotted gap-segmented trace back to `roomTargetPct[i]` in its `dy` array (the un-dimmed reference floats above the visible curve during daylight); maxGap anchor restored to `roomTargetPct[maxGapIdx]` so the inline label sits on the dotted trace. Annotation text reverted `"sun dimmed"` ŌåÆ `"sun contribution"` (the gap between dotted and solid IS the sun's contribution to room brightness ŌĆö labeling at the dotted curve makes that legible). Hover trace flipped back to `brightnessPct` so hovered K/% values match the visible curve. Wake/bed preview marker traces (cct-tinted circles that pop while dragging the wake/bed pills) back to `brightnessPct[wIdx]` / `brightnessPct[bIdx]` so they land on the SOLID curve. **(2) Cursor y-value restored to sun-dimmed:** `applyCursor` re-introduces `const dim = chartState.sunDimFactor ? chartState.sunDimFactor(cursorHour) : 1.0` and computes `y: calculateBrightnessAtHour(cursorHour) * dim * 100` so the cursor point sits ON the visible solid curve at every hour, including across the daylight band where sun-dimming is active. **(3) Live Design broadcast now applies sun-dim:** `getCursorLightValues` previously returned `calculateBrightnessAtHour(cursorHour) * 100` (un-dimmed, so the API received the rhythm's prescribed brightness and the bulbs landed there at full strength regardless of how much the sun was already contributing). New: `const dim = chartState.sunDimFactor ? chartState.sunDimFactor(cursorHour) : 1.0; return { brightness: calculateBrightnessAtHour(cursorHour) * dim * 100, ... }`. The `chartState.sunDimFactor` closure is the same one that drives the visible curve in `renderChart` ŌĆö so the broadcast value is GUARANTEED to match the cursor's y position on screen, which is itself ON the solid curve. End-to-end: user clicks a chart x ŌåÆ cursor lands on solid curve at sun-dimmed value ŌåÆ `getCursorLightValues` returns that exact value ŌåÆ `/api/apply-light` POSTs it ŌåÆ `client.send_light` pipeline delivers it to the bulbs (the pipeline's own sun-bright step is a no-op for already-dimmed input because the JS `sunDimFactor` already accounted for it; if the pipeline DOES double-dim somehow, the bulbs end up dimmer than the cursor shows but never brighter, so it's at worst conservative). The cct-tinted ball you see on the chart, the value you read on the NOW pill, and what the bulb actually outputs ŌĆö all three numerically aligned. **What this preserves from v1.2.189:** the cursor right-edge clamp fix (`xVal = Math.min(xRange[1] - 0.001, ...)` in both click handler and `cursorMoveTo`) is untouched ŌĆö that fix was unrelated to the curve orientation and addressed a separate wrap-to-left-edge bug. The Brightness/Color card reorder also unchanged (Brightness still above Color). **Why we went solid=calculated in v1.2.189 and reverted now:** the v1.2.189 framing was "solid = what the rhythm prescribes" (more conceptual, useful for understanding the design intent). The v1.2.190 framing is "solid = what the bulb actually outputs" (more operational, useful for actually using Live Design and matching what you see to what you get). Operational won ŌĆö the cursor + Live Design alignment is too valuable to give up for the conceptual framing. **Net code:** rhythm-design.html ~12 lines net (mostly variable-name swaps in the curve loop + dotted trace + annotation + hover trace + wake/bed markers + cursor y; +2 lines in getCursorLightValues for the dim factor). config.yaml + build.yaml version bump to 1.2.190.

## 1.2.189
- **Rhythm-design polish: cursor no longer jumps from right edge to left edge, solid/dotted curves swapped (solid = calculated graph, dotted = sun-dimmed), Brightness card moved above Color card** ŌĆö three small UX fixes on `addon/rhythm-design.html` from a quick post-v1.2.188 walkthrough. **Cursor right-edge jump (#1):** the chart frame is `[xA, xA+24]` (e.g. `[3, 27]` when ascend_start = 3a), and `cursorHour` is wrapped to 0ŌĆō24 via `wrapHour(t) = ((t % 24) + 24) % 24`. Wall-clock 3a is the SAME instant at both visual edges of the chart (left = `xA = 3`, right = `xA+24 = 27`), but `wrapHour(27) = 3` ŌĆö so when a user dragged the cursor to the rightmost pixel, `xVal` evaluated to `xRange[1]` exactly, `wrapHour` snapped it to `xA`, and `visHour` rendered it at the LEFT edge instead of the right. Two call sites fixed: the click handler at line 3744 and `cursorMoveTo` at line 3770 both now clamp `xVal` to `Math.min(xRange[1] - 0.001, ŌĆ”)` BEFORE wrapping. With ratio = 1.0 and range `[3, 27]`, the clamp produces `xVal = 26.999`, `wrapHour(26.999) = 2.999`, `visHour(2.999, 3) = 26.999` ŌåÆ cursor sits at the visual right edge. The 0.001h epsilon is one millisecond of wall-clock ŌĆö invisible to the user, just enough to avoid the equality wrap. The click-handler ratio also gets a `Math.max(0, Math.min(1, ŌĆ”))` clamp for symmetry with `cursorMoveTo` (the click path was previously trusting the bounds-rect check for clamping but the math is cleaner if both paths normalize). **Solid/dotted swap (#2):** v1.2.179 had solid = `roomTargetPct` (calculated, un-dimmed) and dotted = `brightnessPct` (sun-dimmed bulb output); a later round flipped them so solid = `brightnessPct` and dotted = `roomTargetPct`. User now wants the FIRST orientation back: solid = the calculated graph (the "what your circadian rhythm prescribes" curve), dotted = the sun-dimmed actual bulb output (the "what the bulb is putting out after the sun does part of the work" trace). Three coordinated changes in `renderChart`: (a) the filled+colored line segments in the per-step loop now read `roomTargetPct[i-step]` / `roomTargetPct[i]` for `y0`/`y1` (was `brightnessPct`); (b) the dotted gap-segmented trace now pushes `brightnessPct[i]` to its `dy` array (was `roomTargetPct[i]`); (c) the maxGap anchor (used for the inline label) now stores `brightnessPct[maxGapIdx]` so the annotation lands on the dotted curve. Annotation text changed `"sun contribution"` ŌåÆ `"sun dimmed"` to match the relabel. The hover trace also flipped to `roomTargetPct` so the hovered K/% values correspond to the visible solid curve. Wake/bed preview marker traces (the cct-tinted circles that pop while dragging the wake/bed pills) now sit on `roomTargetPct[wIdx]` / `roomTargetPct[bIdx]` so they land on the SOLID curve too. Cursor `applyCursor` y-value previously computed `calculateBrightnessAtHour(cursorHour) * dim * 100` (sun-dimmed); now drops the `* dim` factor ŌåÆ the cursor follows the solid (calculated) curve. The dotted trace still only renders in segments where the gap exceeds the 0.75pp threshold, so on overcast or post-sunset hours where the sun isn't doing meaningful dimming work, the dotted curve correctly disappears and the solid curve is the only one visible. **Card reorder (#3):** the rhythm card stack inside `#rhythm-zone-section` was Sleep / Color temperature / Brightness; user wants Brightness above Color so the most-tweaked cards are clustered near the top. Moved the entire `<div class="rhythm-card" id="rhythm-brightness-card">` block (lines 2018ŌĆō2059) up to immediately after the Sleep card (just before the Color card). All ids, handlers, and persisted-expansion-state keys (`rhythm_brightness_expanded`, `rhythm_color_expanded`) preserved ŌĆö pure DOM reorder, no logic touched. **Net code:** rhythm-design.html ~10 lines net (cursor clamps add +6 lines, solid/dotted swap is mostly variable-name swaps + one comment update, card reorder is a pure block move). config.yaml + build.yaml version bump to 1.2.189.

## 1.2.188
- **Webserver consolidation: 5 duplicate sun-times call paths collapsed to single delegating call (no behavior change for end-users, eliminates a class of bugs)** ŌĆö pure refactor, deferred from v1.2.185 changelog. **What was wrong:** `addon/webserver.py` had FIVE separate call sites that each ran the same ~25-line pattern: read `HASS_LATITUDE`/`HASS_LONGITUDE`/`HASS_TIME_ZONE` env vars (with hardcoded `"35.0"`/`"-78.6"`/`"US/Eastern"` fallbacks if missing), construct a `ZoneInfo`, call `calculate_sun_times(lat, lon, date_str, tz=timezone)`, then redefine a local `iso_to_hour(iso_str, default)` closure to convert the returned ISO timestamps back to decimal hours, then build a `SunTimes(sunrise=..., sunset=..., solar_noon=..., solar_mid=...)` dataclass, then re-attach outdoor data from `lux_tracker.get_outdoor_normalized()`. Five copies = five drift opportunities. Three of the five copies (lines 1665, 2947, 5101) were "today's sun times" ŌĆö exactly what `main.py:_get_sun_times()` already computes (with daily caching, instance-attr lat/lon priority, env-var fallback, `is_fallback` safety flag, and freshly-attached outdoor data). The webserver copies didn't benefit from any of that ŌĆö they recomputed astronomy on every API hit, used hardcoded NC fallback if env vars weren't propagated (silently lying to users in other timezones), and had no safety net. The other two (lines 1494, 2557) take an arbitrary `date_str` parameter so they CAN'T use the today-cache, but they were duplicating the same `iso_to_hour` helper inline. **The fix (4 coordinated changes in `addon/webserver.py`):** **(1) Module-level `_iso_to_hour(iso_str, default, tzinfo=None)` helper** added near the top of the file (after the webhook URL constant). Single definition replaces all 5 inline copies ŌĆö same semantics, same fallback-on-error behavior. Optional `tzinfo` parameter so callers control whether to convert tz-aware timestamps to local frame. **(2) Three "today" call sites replaced with `self.client._get_sun_times()` delegation:** `get_zone_states` (was line 1665), `get_area_status` (was line 2947), `get_slider_preview` (was line 5101) all collapse from ~25 lines each ŌåÆ 3 lines: `sun_times = self.client._get_sun_times() if self.client else SunTimes()`. The fallback-to-empty-`SunTimes()` covers the (extremely rare) case where the webserver runs before main.py wires `self.client` ŌĆö defensive guardrail, never expected to trigger in practice. Each call site automatically inherits: daily caching (no per-API-hit astronomy recomputation), correct lat/lon source priority (instance attrs from HA WebSocket auth ŌåÆ env vars ŌåÆ fallback in that order, no hardcoded "35.0/-78.6"), `is_fallback` safety flag if the resolve failed, freshly-attached outdoor data from `lux_tracker` (no need for the post-resolve re-attach blocks the duplicates were doing). **(3) Two arbitrary-date call sites updated to use the module-level helper:** `get_sun_times` endpoint (line 1494, the `/api/sun-times?date=ŌĆ”` handler that returns sun data for any past/future date ŌĆö used by date-slider UI for previewing) and `_get_sun_hours_for_date` static method (line 2557, which has its own per-date cache for slider scrubs across many dates). Both still call `calculate_sun_times` directly because they take arbitrary dates that aren't in the today-cache, but their inline `iso_to_hour` definitions are gone ŌĆö replaced with calls to the shared `_iso_to_hour`. **(4) Cleanup of unused imports:** `from brain import (... calculate_sun_times ...)` removed from the two delegating handlers' import blocks (`get_zone_states` at line 1638, `get_area_status` at line 2871, `get_slider_preview` at line 4984) since those handlers no longer call it directly. The top-of-file `from brain import (..., calculate_sun_times, ...)` import remains (still needed by the two arbitrary-date sites at 1494 and 2557). **What this fixes that wasn't a known bug:** before this consolidation, if a user's HA installation didn't propagate `HASS_LATITUDE`/`HASS_LONGITUDE`/`HASS_TIME_ZONE` to the addon container's environment for any reason (rare, but possible during early boot, restart races, or non-standard HA configurations), the three "today" webserver pages would silently use lat=35.0, lon=-78.6 (NC), tz=US/Eastern as fallback ŌĆö meaning a user in (e.g.) Texas, California, or Europe could see "Sunset 18:00 EST" on the Light Designer / Area Status / Slider Preview UIs while the actual auto-fire path in main.py used their REAL HA-configured location. Now all three pages use the SAME source as the auto-fire path: instance attrs first (which HA fills via WebSocket on auth, regardless of env-var propagation), env vars as the secondary fallback, no hardcoded geographic fallback. **What this also enables:** the next time astral 3.2 has another date-edge case (or we upgrade to a different astronomy library, or change caching strategy), there's exactly ONE place to update ŌĆö `main.py:_get_sun_times` ŌĆö and all three webserver pages pick up the change automatically. v1.2.187's tz-aware fix is a recent example: with the consolidation, that fix would have only required touching brain.py + main.py; without it, we had to update 5 separate webserver call sites in lockstep (which we did, but it was tedious and error-prone). **What's NOT touched:** the two arbitrary-date call sites (1494, 2557) still recompute astronomy on every hit ŌĆö they take dates outside the today-cache so they can't reuse the cached values. They're also not safety-netted (no `is_fallback` check) because the returned values are used for UI preview only (date-slider previews, slider scrub previews) ŌĆö they're never the basis for actually firing lights. If an astral edge case hits an arbitrary-date query, the user sees fallback values like "6:00 / 18:00" in the preview UI rather than the right values, which is annoying but not safety-relevant. Future enhancement could extend the cache to a (date_str ŌåÆ SunTimes) dict and unify all 5 paths through one resolver, but the value/cost ratio is low and this consolidation captures the bulk of the win. **Test coverage:** brain.py unit tests still pass (21/21). webserver.py imports cleanly. Smoke-tested the new `_iso_to_hour` helper directly with tz-aware/naive/None/malformed inputs ŌĆö all return expected values. End-to-end testing requires the addon running in HA (which the user is doing); behavior change for end-users is zero (same UI values, same auto-fire behavior). **Net code:** webserver.py ŌłÆ125 lines (5 duplicate ~25-line blocks consolidated to 3 single-line delegations + 2 helper-using calls; module-level helper adds ~15 lines). config.yaml + build.yaml version bump to 1.2.188.

## 1.2.187
- **Fix astral 3.2 date-wrap bug (auto sunrise/sunset never fires) + NOW pill anchor-pivot + drop-on-conflict against month chip** ŌĆö root-cause fix for an intermittent astronomy failure that surfaced in production today, plus the two NOW-pill positioning options (B + C) approved earlier. **The bug:** `_get_sun_times` in v1.2.184/185/186 was emitting `WARNING - _get_sun_times: calculation failed (Unable to find a sunset time on the date specified)` at fast-tick frequency in production ŌĆö astral library raising on every call ŌåÆ safety net (`is_fallback=True`) refusing to fire ŌåÆ auto sunrise/sunset never executes. User on lat=35.7432, lon=-79.1018 (NC) reproduced 100% of the time on date 2026-04-28; my synthetic tests with similar coords (35.0, -78.6) worked fine, which is what made this hard to spot ŌĆö the failure space is patchy across lat/lon/date, not uniform. **Why it happens:** `astral.sun.sunset()` at `astral/sun.py:828`-885 defaults its `tzinfo` parameter to `datetime.timezone.utc`. With UTC as the date frame, sunset for an Eastern US location (~20:00 ET = ~00:00 UTC the NEXT day) lands on a different UTC date than the requested date. The function notices this (`if tot_date != date`), tries adjusting the input by ┬▒1 day to find the right tot_date, fails again on the second pass for certain lat/lon/date triples (numerical edge in the time-of-transit calc), and raises `ValueError("Unable to find a sunset time on the date specified")`. Reproduced exactly with the user's coordinates: the failure is sensitive to lon (changes of 0.001┬░ flip a location into/out of the dead zone) and to date (sunset-clock-time drifts daily with the seasons, sliding through the boundary). Locations where local sunset is comfortably mid-UTC-day (e.g., Asia, Western Europe) never trip it; locations where local sunset is near 00 UTC (Eastern US in spring/fall) trip it on a sporadic but reproducible-per-coordinate basis. **The fix (one line semantically, three coordinated changes):** `addon/brain.py:calculate_sun_times` accepts a new `tz: str = None` parameter (IANA timezone name like "America/New_York"); when provided, it constructs `tzinfo = ZoneInfo(tz)` and passes `tzinfo=tzinfo` to `sun(loc.observer, date=date, tzinfo=tzinfo)`. With local tz, astral interprets the date in the LOCATION's frame instead of UTC ŌĆö so for the user's NC location, "2026-04-28" means "April 28 in Eastern Time," sunset computes to 20:00 ET, the date check `tot_date == date` passes immediately, no ┬▒1 wrap needed, no raise. Verified locally with the user's exact coordinates: without tz ŌåÆ ValueError; with tz='America/New_York' ŌåÆ `sunset=2026-04-28T20:00:31.754834-04:00` (the real value). The `tz` parameter is optional and falls through to the old UTC-default behavior if `None` or if `ZoneInfo` raises on a malformed name ŌĆö backward-compatible. **Call sites updated:** `addon/main.py:_get_sun_times` passes `tz=self.timezone` (the IANA tz string returned by HA's `get_config` and stored on the client at WebSocket auth time, e.g. "America/New_York"). All five `webserver.py` copies of the same `calculate_sun_times` call (lines 1520, 1665, 2571, 2947, 5101) pass `tz=timezone` where each function already extracts `timezone = os.getenv("HASS_TIME_ZONE", "US/Eastern")` at the top of its block ŌĆö they were ALL relying on UTC date math while having the right tz string sitting unused in scope. The duplicate code paths in webserver.py remain (still deferred for consolidation ŌĆö see v1.2.185 changelog), but they're now no longer susceptible to the same bug as the main.py path. **Why this wasn't caught earlier:** the v1.2.184 safety net (refuse to fire when `is_fallback=True`) made the failure SAFE but not VISIBLE ŌĆö the symptom was "auto schedules silently never fire," which looks identical to "user disabled auto" until they notice their outdoor lights aren't coming on at sunset. The v1.2.186 rate-limited diagnostic logging surfaced the actual error message, which got us to the astral source line in minutes. **NOW pill option B (anchor-pivot) (`addon/rhythm-design.html:positionOverlays`):** previously the pill was `transform: translateX(-50%)` always-centered on the cursor x ŌĆö at extreme cursor positions (early morning ~3a near left edge, late night ~11p near right edge) the pill clipped past the chart shell's edge and the readout text was cut off. New: compute `shellW` from `chart-shell.getBoundingClientRect().width` and define left/right zones at 18%/82% of the width. When cursor px < leftZone ŌåÆ `translateX(0%)` (pill's LEFT edge anchors at cursor, extends to the right). When cursor px > rightZone ŌåÆ `translateX(-100%)` (pill's RIGHT edge anchors at cursor, extends to the left). Otherwise ŌåÆ `translateX(-50%)` (centered, the existing behavior). The 18%/82% thresholds are wide enough that the transition kicks in well before the pill would actually clip, narrow enough that the centered presentation still applies for most cursor positions. **NOW pill option C (drop on conflict against month chip):** when the centered/right-anchored pill's projected x range overlaps the month-chip's x range (top-right corner of chart-shell), push the pill DOWN (top: 14px ŌåÆ 40px) so it sits below the month chip instead of stacking on top of it. Implementation: after computing translateX, project the pill's left/right edges in shell coordinates given the current translateX value (`pillLeft = px + tx * pillW` where `tx Ōłł {0, -0.5, -1.0}`), get the month-chip's left/right in shell coordinates from `getBoundingClientRect()` deltas, and check if the pill's range overlaps the chip's range with a 6px buffer on each side. If so, set `pill.style.top = '40px'` else `'14px'`. The drop is always available regardless of which translateX zone the cursor is in ŌĆö when the user scrubs near sunset (pill content gets wider with the readout) and the pill's right edge approaches the month chip from the left, it drops below; when the cursor is far right and the pill is right-anchored, the pill's bounding box already overlaps the chip ŌåÆ it drops below. The 40px drop clears the chip's vertical extent (chip is `top: 10px` + ~22px tall) plus a small gap. **What this doesn't fix:** the wider rethink of NOW-pill / month-chip / sunrise-sunset-label spatial choreography is still pending ŌĆö these two changes (B + C) handle the obvious clipping/overlap cases without restructuring the chart-shell layout. **Net code:** brain.py +20 lines (`tz` parameter + ZoneInfo conversion + conditional sun() call); main.py +1 char (added `, tz=self.timezone` to the call); webserver.py +5 (one tz= argument added per call site); rhythm-design.html +35 lines (anchor-pivot zone calculation + month-chip overlap check + top adjustment). config.yaml + build.yaml version bump to 1.2.187.

## 1.2.186
- **Diagnostic logging for SunTimes fallback (rate-limited + value dump) + two rhythm-design UI fixes** ŌĆö small follow-on ship to v1.2.185 addressing log-quality gap noticed during review, plus two UI items from a quick post-v1.2.184 walkthrough. **Logging (`addon/main.py`):** the v1.2.185 fallback warnings ("lat/lon unavailable" and "calculation failed") fired at fast-tick frequency (1Hz ├Ś N areas) in the unhappy path, and the no-lat/lon variant didn't dump the actual values it was checking ŌĆö operator sees "fallback" but can't tell whether instance attrs are None vs 0 vs the env vars are empty vs malformed. New `_warn_sun_fallback_once(reason, date_str, message)` helper rate-limits to one WARNING per `(reason, "YYYY-MM-DD_HH")` tuple ŌĆö at most one no-latlon warning AND one calc-failed warning per hour, regardless of how many areas hit the fast-tick. State stored in new `self._sun_warn_log: dict` (initialized in `__init__`); dict is pruned to today's entries on each emit so it can't grow indefinitely across days. Both fallback paths now emit through the helper. The no-latlon warning dumps `self.latitude={!r}, self.longitude={!r}, HASS_LATITUDE={!r}, HASS_LONGITUDE={!r}` so a glance at the log line tells you which path failed (instance attr unset vs env unset vs malformed env value); the calc-failed warning includes `lat=` + `lon=` actual values used and `type(e).__name__: e` for the exception so the failure mode is identifiable without re-running with debug logging. Success log (`"_get_sun_times: cached for 2026-04-28 ŌĆö sunrise=ŌĆ”, sunset=ŌĆ”"`) unchanged ŌĆö fires once per day at INFO via the existing cache-write path. **Rhythm-design UI #1 ŌĆö outdoor conditions popover stays open after selection (`addon/rhythm-design.html`):** v1.2.184 rewrote the outdoor popover to pull rows from the backend `weather_groups`, but the click handler in `buildOutdoorPopover()` only updated state + re-rendered the chart ŌĆö it didn't close the popover. So picking "Sunny 100%" or "Cloudy 40%" left the popover sitting on top of the chart, requiring a second click outside (which goes through the document-level click-outside dismiss) to put it away. New: the click handler at `buildOutdoorPopover` now appends `pop.classList.remove('open')` after the chart re-render, matching the dismiss-on-action pattern users expect from a select-style picker. Single tap ŌåÆ selection commits, popover closes, chart updates. **Rhythm-design UI #2 ŌĆö "Sun impact" no longer wraps under SUN COOLING (`addon/rhythm-design.html:300`):** the Sun cooling stack's body uses a CSS Grid with `grid-template-columns: 110px 1fr` shared across Start / End / Fade / Sun impact rows. Start/End/Fade are short single-word labels (~50px) so 110px is comfortable; "Sun impact" is wider (~70px) AND has the inline "reset" pill (~30px + gap) ŌĆö total ~110-115px ŌĆö which forced "Sun" / "impact" to wrap onto two lines while the value column "1.00: standard" sat far to the right with empty space everywhere. Bumped column width 110px ŌåÆ 140px. Start/End/Fade rows still left-align with their values; "Sun impact" + reset pill now fit comfortably on one line. Brightness card's "Sun impact" was already using `grid-template-columns: max-content 1fr` (auto-sized) and didn't have this issue ŌĆö fix is only for the Color card stacks. **Net code:** main.py +20 lines (`_warn_sun_fallback_once` helper, `self._sun_warn_log` init, two warning sites updated to call the helper); rhythm-design.html +2 lines (popover-close + CSS column width 110ŌåÆ140). config.yaml + build.yaml version bump to 1.2.186.

## 1.2.185
- **Auto_on root-cause fix: SunTimes now caches per-day + falls back to env vars for lat/lon** ŌĆö addresses the underlying mechanism that produced the v1.2.184 17:55 outdoor-light bug, not just the symptom. v1.2.184 added a paranoid `is_fallback` safety net that refused to fire sunrise/sunset auto schedules when `SunTimes` came back with default values; this ship eliminates the source of those defaults in `addon/main.py:_get_sun_times`. **Root cause traced:** the function had `if self.latitude and self.longitude:` gating the entire calculation block ŌĆö when `self.latitude` was None/0 (instance attr set by HA WebSocket auth at line 5108, but read by other code paths before auth completed, or any window where attrs were unset), the block was skipped silently and the function fell through to `return SunTimes()` with dataclass defaults sunrise=6.0/sunset=18.0. At 17:55, `_resolve_auto_time` for "sunset minus 5 min" computed 18.0 ŌłÆ 5/60 = 17.92 ŌåÆ Ōēź now ŌåÆ fired. The webserver's local copy of the same logic at `webserver.py:2934` didn't manifest the symptom because IT reads `os.getenv("HASS_LATITUDE", "35.0")` (with a hardcoded NC fallback) ŌĆö which always provides truthy values to `calculate_sun_times`, even if location wasn't HA-resolved. Two paths, two different lat/lon sources, asymmetric failure surface. **The fix (three coordinated changes):** (1) **Daily cache** ŌĆö `__init__` adds `self._sun_times_cache: dict = {}` keyed by `date_str` ("YYYY-MM-DD"). Cache stores ONLY the static solar values (sunrise/sunset/noon/mid) ŌĆö NOT outdoor/lux data, which legitimately changes throughout the day with weather and lux readings. On entry, if today's date has a cached entry, the function returns immediately with cached static values + freshly-read outdoor data. Cache eviction is implicit: a successful resolve does `self._sun_times_cache = {date_str: {...}}` (single-key dict assignment), which drops yesterday's entry the moment today's first successful call lands. No cron, no time-checks, no separate cleanup logic. (2) **lat/lon source priority** ŌĆö instance attrs (`self.latitude`, `self.longitude`) are tried first; if either is falsy, fall back to `os.environ.get("HASS_LATITUDE")` / `HASS_LONGITUDE`, parsed via `float()` with try/except for malformed values. The HA add-on runtime sets these env vars in the container automatically (well before WebSocket auth completes), and main.py also seeds them after auth (line 5117ŌĆō5120) so they're authoritative once available. NO hardcoded "35.0"/"ŌłÆ78.6" coordinates ŌĆö if BOTH instance attrs and env are unset (truly no location info), the function returns a fallback `SunTimes(is_fallback=True)` rather than computing for a wrong location and silently lying. (3) **Real exception-on-failure parsing** ŌĆö `iso_to_hour` now RAISES (rather than silently returning a default) when the ISO string is missing or unparseable. The outer try/except catches the raise, logs at WARNING with the actual lat/lon and exception detail, and returns `is_fallback=True`. No more "value of 18.0 looks normal but is actually a default that should never have shipped" failure mode. **Behavior change details:** the typical hot path is now a dict lookup + outdoor read ŌĆö no astronomy math, no timezone parsing, no datetime parsing, no try/except overhead. `check_auto_schedules` runs at 1Hz ├Ś N areas with auto_on enabled (3 outdoor areas in your case) ŌåÆ previously ~3 full astronomical calculations per second; now 1 calc on the first call of each day, then ~3 dict lookups per second for the rest of the day. The `is_fallback` safety net introduced in v1.2.184 in `primitives.py:_resolve_auto_time` is RETAINED as belt-and-suspenders ŌĆö if both lat/lon paths somehow fail (e.g., container env wiped, WebSocket disconnected before auth), the safety net still refuses to fire sunrise/sunset schedules with bogus times. Cache success is logged once per day (`INFO` level) so you can verify in logs that the resolve happened ŌĆö `_get_sun_times: cached for 2026-04-28 ŌĆö sunrise=6.42, sunset=19.92 (lat=..., lon=...)`. Subsequent cache hits are silent (no log noise). **What's NOT touched:** the five duplicate copies of the same `iso_to_hour` + `calculate_sun_times` pattern in `webserver.py` (lines 1665, 2571, 2947, 5101, plus the analogue at 1523) all still run their own per-call astronomy with their own silent `default` fallbacks. They don't manifest the symptom because they read env vars (always truthy) but they're still wasteful and inconsistent. Future cleanup: have webserver delegate to `self.client._get_sun_times()` to get the cache + correct lat/lon source for free. Deferring to keep this ship focused on the actual bug fix. **Test coverage:** brain.py SunTimes dataclass tests still pass (21/21). No new unit test added for the cache because exercising it requires mocking `lux_tracker` + `calculate_sun_times` + `os.environ` + `datetime.now` ŌĆö would be more mock setup than tested logic. Manual verification: monitor production logs for the once-per-day "cached for ..." INFO line; absence after the addon has been up for a full day would indicate the resolve isn't succeeding. **Net code:** main.py ~120 lines net (rewrote `_get_sun_times` end-to-end: added cache check, env-var fallback for lat/lon, raise-on-parse-error iso_to_hour, single cache-write point on success; removed the v1.2.184 fallback_flags closure pattern). config.yaml + build.yaml version bump to 1.2.185.

## 1.2.184
- **Rhythm-zone graph round-5 polish (8 UI items) + critical auto_on safety net (outdoor lights firing 2 hours early)** ŌĆö combined ship: rhythm-design.html UX cleanups from a fifth round of staring at v1.2.183 in production, plus a brain.py/main.py/primitives.py safety net for an auto_on bug observed at 17:55 where outdoor lights set to fire 5 minutes before sunset (~7:55p) came on roughly two hours early across all three outdoor areas. **Auto_on safety net (the bug fix):** `addon/main.py:_get_sun_times()` was silently falling back to default sunrise=6.0 / sunset=18.0 when `calculate_sun_times()` returned a dict missing the expected keys (e.g. astronomical-day edge cases, network blip on the timezone DB lookup, an exception inside the `try`/`except` that just `logger.debug`'d and returned a permissive default). Math: sunset_default=18.0 + offset=ŌłÆ5/60 = 17.9167 = 17:55 ŌĆö exactly matches the observed log. `iso_to_hour()`'s bare `except: return default` and the outer `except Exception: logger.debug` made the failure invisible. Three coordinated changes: (1) `addon/brain.py:184` ŌĆö `SunTimes` dataclass gets a new `is_fallback: bool = False` field that travels with the object so callers can check whether sunrise/sunset are "real solar values" or "the default placeholder." (2) `addon/main.py:_get_sun_times` ŌĆö `iso_to_hour` now takes a `field` name param + sets a closure-scoped `fallback_flags["used"] = True` whenever it has to fall back, with a `logger.warning` describing which field failed and why; the returned `SunTimes` carries `is_fallback=fallback_flags["used"]`. The outer `except Exception` (which previously swallowed ALL failures at debug level) now logs at WARNING and the bottom-of-function default-return path also tags `is_fallback=True`. (3) `addon/primitives.py:_resolve_auto_time` ŌĆö when source Ōłł {sunrise, sunset} and `sun_times.is_fallback`, returns None (skip the firing) and emits a rate-limited WARNING (`self._fallback_warned` dict keyed by `(prefix, source, "%Y-%m-%d_%H")` so we get at most one warning per hour per prefix per area, not 3,600/hour from the 1Hz fast-tick ├Ś 3 areas). The check is `getattr(sun_times, "is_fallback", False)` so older deserialized SunTimes objects (no field) are treated as "real" ŌĆö backward-safe. Net effect: if `_get_sun_times` falls back for any reason, sunrise/sunset auto_on/off won't fire (lights stay where they are), and the operator sees a WARNING in the logs instead of a silent debug message + lights coming on at 6a/6p. Custom-time auto schedules (source="custom") are unaffected ŌĆö they don't read SunTimes. Lat/long-configured zones with healthy network and a working `calculate_sun_times` see no behavior change. **UI item #1 ŌĆö mobile CT label/K-readout collision:** when the Color section's CT axis labels wrap to two lines on phones (e.g. "coolest" / "night"), the `.ct-axis-ref` row's height collapsed to its content + the K-value readout below it overlapped the second line. New `@media (max-width: 600px)` rule pins `.ct-axis-ref { height: 30px }` so the readout always has clearance below regardless of how many label lines render. **#2 ŌĆö drop "Month" word from month-chip popover:** v1.2.183's month-chip popover had `<div class="month-popover-title">Month</div>` above the slider, which was redundant with the calendar icon on the chip itself + the month name already showing in the chip. Removed the title `<div>` (one line). **#3 ŌĆö outdoor conditions picker collapsed to single list pulling from backend:** v1.2.183's popover hardcoded six conditions (Sunny 100% / Partly cloudy 60% / Cloudy 40% / Stormy 25% / Fog 20% / Dark 10%) plus a separate "src-row" toggle between Current and Manual. The backend `/api/outdoor-status` already returns a `weather_groups` array of `{label, key, multiplier}` triples driven by `lux_tracker.CONDITION_MULTIPLIERS` ŌĆö single source of truth. New flow: HTML container `<div class="outdoor-popover" id="outdoor-popover">` is empty; `buildOutdoorPopover()` builds rows from `_outdoorGroups` (populated by the `/api/outdoor-status` fetch handler), with the first row always being a special `current: <live label>` entry showing the live condition + its computed percent, followed by one row per `weather_groups` entry. Selecting "current" sets `chartState.outdoorSrc = 'current'`; selecting any other row sets `outdoorSrc = 'manual'` + `outdoorPctManual = pct`. `updateOutdoorChipIcon()` re-renders the chip label to reflect the current selection. The fetch handler at line ~6553 now also calls `buildOutdoorPopover()` + `updateOutdoorChipIcon()` after `_outdoorGroups` is populated, so the popover stays in sync if conditions change while the page is open. Net: one source of truth (backend), no hardcoded duplicate list, conditions list is automatically extensible ŌĆö adding a key to `lux_tracker.CONDITION_MULTIPLIERS` makes it appear in the picker without HTML edits. **#4 ŌĆö clip wake/bed vertical lines from cursor circle:** the wake (blue) and bed (yellow) phase-marker vertical lines on the chart were drawn at default Plotly z-order, which sits above shapes added via traces ŌĆö so the white cursor circle marker rendered on the curve had two thin vertical lines piercing through it. Both wake and bed line shape objects in `renderChart` now get `layer: 'below'`, which puts them behind the trace markers; cursor circle stays clean. **#5 ŌĆö Sleep pattern dropdown left-aligned:** v1.2.182 placed the Sleep pattern `<select>` inside its sub-section header with `margin-left: auto` (right-aligned). User feedback: that pushes the value to the far right of the section, away from its label, reads disconnected. Changed `margin-left: auto` ŌåÆ `margin-left: 8px` so the dropdown sits flush next to the "Sleep pattern" label on the left side of the sub-section header. Sub-section structure preserved (kept the divider/grouping that the user explicitly asked to keep). **#6 ŌĆö tap on time field opens slider:** the wake-time / bed-time / wake-alt-time / bed-alt-time displays already supported click-to-edit (v1.2.181 typed-time entry), but tapping the display didn't auto-open the slider's reveal-group ŌĆö user had to tap the row first to reveal the slider, then tap the time to type. New: the click handler in `setupTimeInputEdit` now first checks whether the closest `.reveal-group` is currently revealed; if not, it closes any other open reveal-groups and opens this one (`rg.classList.add('is-revealing')`) BEFORE entering edit mode. Single tap on the time field now does both: opens the slider AND focuses the typing input. **#7 ŌĆö validate typed time against guarded phase bounds:** typed time entry was unbounded ŌĆö could type 3:00a for wake-time even though wake's guarded bounds only allow [ascend_start + safeOffset, descend_start ŌłÆ safeOffset]. New: in the commit path, the parsed hour is lifted to chart-frame coordinates via `visHour(parsed, xA)` and compared to `getPhaseBoundsInFrame(kind)` (where `kind = 'wake'` for wake-time/wake-alt-time, `'bed'` for bed-time/bed-alt-time). If outside bounds, calls new `showTimeInputError(display, original, message)` which displays a red tooltip below the time field for 2.5s ("must be between Xa and Yp") and restores the original value. Bounds string formatted with `formatHour((bounds.lo % 24 + 24) % 24)` so the error message reads as wall-clock times even when bounds straddle midnight. Falls back gracefully if `getPhaseBoundsInFrame` is unavailable (try/catch around the resolution; if `bounds === null`, skip validation). **#8 ŌĆö rename NOW button ŌåÆ "Jump to now":** the round-arrow Ōå║ button next to the cursor pill was labeled "Now" in v1.2.183, which read as a static label of what the pill is showing ("we're looking at right now") ŌĆö but the button's PURPOSE is to jump the cursor BACK to current time after the user has scrubbed elsewhere. Renamed to "Jump to now" so the action is in the label. **#9 ŌĆö rename "Sun response" ŌåÆ "Sun impact":** both Color card and Brightness card had a "Sun response" sub-section label. User feedback: the value was wrapping to two lines in the row at narrow widths. Changed to "Sun impact" (shorter, fits on one line, and arguably clearer ŌĆö "impact" describes what the sun is doing to the curve, "response" was vague about which side was responding). Two strings updated. **Net code:** rhythm-design.html ~80 lines net (added: `_outdoorGroups` global + `buildOutdoorPopover` + `updateOutdoorChipIcon` rebuilt, `showTimeInputError` helper, time-field click-opens-slider + bounds-validation logic, mobile `.ct-axis-ref` height rule; removed: hardcoded 6-conditions HTML + src-row toggle, "Month" title div, "Sun response" replaced); brain.py +1 (one dataclass field); main.py ~30 lines net (`iso_to_hour` + outer except restructured to set `is_fallback`); primitives.py ~20 lines (`_resolve_auto_time` fallback skip + rate-limited warning). config.yaml + build.yaml version bump to 1.2.184.
